    <div style="margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 6pt"><table cellpadding="0" cellspacing="0" style="border-collapse: collapse; width: 100%; font-size: 10pt"><tr style="vertical-align: top; text-align: left"><td style="width: 33%">&#160;</td><td style="width: 34%; text-align: center">&#160;</td><td style="width: 33%">&#160;</td></tr></table></div>

<p style="font: 10pt/15pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><b>&#160;</b></p>

<p style="font: 10pt/15pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><b>ITEM 2.03.</b>&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;<b>Creation of a Direct
Financial Obligation or an Obligation under an Off-Balance Sheet Arrangement of a Registrant.</b></p>

<p style="font: 10pt/15pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><b>&#160;</b></p>

<p style="font: 10pt/15pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify">Boston Scientific
Corporation (&#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline">Boston Scientific</span>&#8221;) submitted a borrowing request for $2.0 billion to be funded on August
19, 2019, under its Term Loan Credit Agreement with the lenders from time to time party thereto, and Barclays Bank PLC
as administrative agent, consisting of a $1.0 billion two-year delayed draw term loan credit facility and a $1.0
billion three-year delayed draw term loan credit facility. The funds from the drawdown will be used to partially finance
Boston Scientific&#8217;s acquisition of BTG plc (&#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline">BTG</span>&#8221;), as described below. Borrowings under the
two-year delayed draw term loan credit facility will mature two years from the date of the closing of the BTG acquisition
and borrowings under the three-year delayed draw term loan credit facility will mature three years from the date of the
closing of the BTG acquisition. For more information regarding the Term Loan Credit Agreement, see Items 1.01, 2.03 and 9.01
in Boston Scientific&#8217;s <a href="http://www.sec.gov/Archives/edgar/data/885725/000094787118000985/ss119647_8k.htm">Form 8-K</a> filed with the Securities and Exchange Commission on December 21, 2018, which
includes such agreement as Exhibit 10.3. Such description and exhibit are incorporated in this Item 2.03 by reference.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt/15pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><b>&#160;</b></p>

<p style="font: 10pt/15pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><b>ITEM 8.01.</b>&#160;&#160;&#160;&#160;<b>Other Events.</b></p>

<p style="font: 12pt/15pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt/15pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify">On August 19, 2019, Boston Scientific,
BTG and Bravo Bidco Limited (&#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline">Bidco</span>&#8221;), an indirect wholly-owned subsidiary of Boston Scientific, issued an announcement
on the London-based Regulatory News Service (&#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline">RNS</span>&#8221;), announcing that the previously announced scheme of arrangement
under Part 26 of the United Kingdom Companies Act 2006, as amended (the &#8220;<span style="text-decoration: underline">Scheme</span>&#8221;) has become effective in accordance
with its terms. Pursuants to the Scheme, Bidco has acquired the entire issued share capital of BTG.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt/15pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt/15pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify">On August 19, 2019, Boston Scientific
also issued a press release, disclosing that BTG has become a wholly-owned subsidiary of Boston Scientific and BTG shares no longer
trade on the London Stock Exchange. Under the terms of the Scheme, holders of BTG common shares will receive 840 pence in cash
per ordinary share of BTG that they hold.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt/15pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt/15pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify">Additionally, Boston Scientific announced
that in due course, it expects to complete the previously announced sale of its global embolic microspheres portfolio&#8212;comprised
of Embozene&#174;, Embozene TANDEM&#174; and ONCOZENE&#8482; brands&#8212;to Varian Medical Systems, Inc., a transaction entered
into in connection with obtaining the antitrust clearances required to effect the Scheme.</p>

<p style="font: 10pt/15pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify">&#160;</p>

<p style="font: 10pt/15pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify">Copies of the aforementioned RNS announcement
and press release are attached as Exhibit 99.1 and Exhibit 99.2, respectively, and are incorporated herein by reference; provided,
however, that information on or connected to our website or the website of any third-party hyperlinked from or referenced in the
RNS announcement and press release included as Exhibit 99.1 and Exhibit 99.2, respectively, to this Current Report on Form 8-K
is expressly not incorporated by reference into or intended to be filed as a part of this Current Report on Form 8-K.</p>



<p style="font: 12pt/15pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0">&#160;</p>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt/130% Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align: right">Exhibit 99.1</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt/130% Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt/130% Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align: justify">NOT FOR RELEASE,
PUBLICATION OR DISTRIBUTION IN WHOLE OR IN PART, DIRECTLY OR INDIRECTLY, IN, INTO OR FROM ANY JURISDICTION WHERE TO DO SO
WOULD CONSTITUTE A VIOLATION OF THE RELEVANT LAWS OR REGULATIONS OF SUCH JURISDICTION</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt/130% Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align: justify">FOR IMMEDIATE RELEASE</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt/130% Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align: right">19 August 2019</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt/130% Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align: center">RECOMMENDED CASH OFFER</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt/130% Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align: center">for</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt/130% Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center">BTG PLC</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt/130% Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align: center">(BTG)</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt/130% Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align: center">by</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt/130% Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center">BRAVO BIDCO LIMITED</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt/130% Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center">(Bidco)</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center"><B>a newly incorporated indirect wholly-owned
subsidiary of Boston Scientific Corporation (Boston Scientific)</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 10pt/13pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: center"><B>intended to be effected by means of
a scheme of arrangement under Part 26 of the Companies Act</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt/13pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 12pt 0 0; text-align: justify"><B>Scheme becomes Effective</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt/13pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 12pt 0 0; text-align: justify">On 20 November 2018, the Boards
of Boston Scientific, Bidco and BTG announced that they had reached agreement on the terms of a recommended cash offer by Bidco
for the acquisition of the entire issued and to be issued ordinary share capital of BTG (the <B>Acquisition</B>). As outlined in
that announcement, the Acquisition is to be effected by means of a scheme of arrangement under part 26 of the Companies Act (the
<B>Scheme</B>). On 28 February 2019, the Scheme was approved by the Scheme Shareholders at the Court Meeting.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt/13pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 12pt 0 0; text-align: justify">Boston Scientific, Bidco and BTG
are pleased to announce that all the Conditions set out in the scheme document dated 24 January 2019 (the <B>Scheme Document</B>)
have been satisfied or waived and the Scheme has today become Effective in accordance with its terms. This follows the Court&rsquo;s
sanction of the Scheme at the Court Hearing held on 15 August 2019.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt/13pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 12pt 0 0; text-align: justify">Scheme Shareholders&rsquo; cash
consideration under the terms of the Acquisition will be settled or despatched, or, in the case of any Scheme Shareholder that
holds Scheme Shares in uncertificated form (that is, in CREST), Euroclear UK &amp; Ireland Limited will be instructed to create
an assured payment obligation (provided that Bidco shall be entitled to settle or despatch cash consideration to any Scheme Shareholder
that holds Scheme Shares in CREST if, for any reason, Bidco wishes to do so), by no later than 2 September 2019.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt/13pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 12pt 0 0; text-align: justify">Except as otherwise defined herein,
capitalised terms used but not defined in this announcement have the same meanings as given to them in the Scheme Document.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt/13pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 12pt 0 0; text-align: justify"><B>Suspension and cancellation
of listing and trading</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt/13pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 12pt 0 0; text-align: justify">The listing of BTG Shares on the
premium listing segment of the Official List and the admission to trading of BTG Shares on the London Stock Exchange&rsquo;s Main
Market were suspended with effect from 7.30 a.m. (London time) on 19 August 2019.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt/13pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 12pt 0 0; text-align: justify">BTG further announces that the
listing of BTG Shares on the premium listing segment of the Official List and the admission to trading of BTG Shares on the London
Stock Exchange&rsquo;s Main Market will each be cancelled with effect from 8.00 a.m. (London time) on 20 August 2019.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt/13pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 12pt 0 0; text-align: justify"></P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt/13pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt/13pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0; text-align: justify">BTG further announces that, with effect

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt/130% Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align: right">Exhibit 99.2</P>

<P STYLE="font: bold 10pt/130% Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 0 6pt; text-align: right">&nbsp;</P>



<P STYLE="font: 11pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0 9pt 0 0"><FONT STYLE="font-family: Arial, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; font-size: 7.5pt"><IMG SRC="image_001.jpg" ALT="" STYLE="height: 85.5pt; width: 556.5pt"></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 4.5pt">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 14pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 4.5pt; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="text-transform: uppercase"><B>&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 14pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 4.5pt; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="text-transform: uppercase"><B>boston
scientific CLOSES ACQUISITION OF BTG plc.&#9;</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 14pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 4.5pt; text-align: center"><FONT STYLE="text-transform: uppercase"><B>&nbsp;</B></FONT></P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0 4.5pt; text-indent: 0.5in; text-align: center">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0">MARLBOROUGH, Mass., August 19, 2019 &ndash; Boston Scientific Corporation
(NYSE: BSX) today announced the completion of its acquisition of BTG plc. (LSE:BTG) pursuant to the previously announced scheme
of arrangement. BTG develops and commercializes products used in minimally-invasive procedures targeting cancer and vascular diseases,
as well as specialty pharmaceuticals.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0">BTG has three key businesses, the largest of which is its highly-differentiated
Interventional Medicine portfolio that encompasses interventional oncology therapeutic technologies for patients with liver and
kidney cancers, as well as a vascular portfolio for treatment of deep vein thrombosis, pulmonary embolism, deep venous obstruction
and superficial venous disease.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0">&ldquo;The addition of the BTG Interventional Medicine portfolio
reinforces our category leadership strategy and enables us to offer best-in-class technologies, unparalleled clinical evidence
and a strengthened commercial infrastructure to support physicians treating some of the most challenging diseases impacting patient
health around the world,&rdquo; said Mike Mahoney, chairman and chief executive officer, Boston Scientific. &ldquo;Leveraging the
employee talent and clinical and commercial expertise of these two high-performing organizations will generate continued innovation
and access so that we may advance patient care in ways that neither company could do alone.&rdquo;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0">In addition to the Interventional Medicine product lines, the BTG
portfolio also includes a specialty pharmaceutical business comprised of acute care antidotes to treat overexposure to certain
medications and toxins, and a licensing business that receives royalties related to BTG intellectual property and product license
agreements.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0">Upon the effectiveness of the scheme of arrangement, BTG became
a wholly-owned subsidiary of Boston Scientific, and BTG shares no longer trade on the London Stock Exchange. Under the terms of
the previously announced transaction, holders of BTG common shares will receive 840 pence in cash per share.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0">Boston Scientific expects to complete the previously announced sale
of its global embolic microspheres portfolio &ndash; comprised of Embozene&reg;, Embozene TANDEM&reg; and ONCOZENE&trade; brands
&ndash; to Varian Medical Systems, Inc. in due course, a transaction entered into in connection with obtaining the antitrust clearances
required to complete the BTG transaction.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0">In addition, the company is initiating a process to explore the
divestiture of the royalty stream associated with BTG&rsquo;s Zytiga&reg; licensing arrangements and anticipates closing this divestiture
by the end of 2019.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0">The transaction is expected to be immaterial to adjusted earnings
per share in 2019 as a result of the BTG transaction closing later than originally anticipated, the divestiture of the Boston Scientific
embolic microspheres portfolio, and the treatment of the licensing business as an asset for accounting purposes and its intended
divestiture. The transaction is expected to be four to five cents accretive in 2020 on an adjusted basis, and increasingly accretive
thereafter. On a GAAP basis, the transaction is expected to be less accretive, or more dilutive as the case may be, due to amortization
expense and acquisition-related net charges.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Calibri, Helvetica, Sans-Serif; margin: 0; text-indent: 0.25in">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"></P>

<!-- Field: Page; Sequence: 1 -->
    <DIV STYLE="margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 6pt; border-bottom: Black 2pt solid"><TABLE CELLPADDING="0" CELLSPACING="0" STYLE="border-collapse: collapse; width: 100%; font-size: 10pt"><TR STYLE="vertical-align: top; text-align: left"><TD STYLE="width: 33%">&nbsp;</TD><TD STYLE="width: 34%; text-align: center">&nbsp;</TD><TD STYLE="width: 33%">&nbsp;</TD></TR></TABLE></DIV>
    <DIV STYLE="page-break-before: always; margin-top: 6pt; margin-bottom: 6pt"><P STYLE="margin: 0pt">&nbsp;</P></DIV>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0"><B>About Boston Scientific</B></P>

<P STYLE="font: 11pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0">Boston Scientific transforms lives through innovative medical solutions
that improve the health of patients around the world.&nbsp;As a global medical technology leader for 40 years, we advance science
for life by providing a broad range of high-performance solutions that address unmet patient needs and reduce the cost of healthcare.
For more information, visit <FONT STYLE="color: blue">www.bostonscientific.com</FONT> and connect on <FONT STYLE="color: blue">Twitter</FONT>
and <FONT STYLE="color: blue">Facebook</FONT>.</P>

<P STYLE="font: 10.5pt HelveticaNeue; margin: 0 4.5pt 0 0">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 4.5pt 0 0; text-align: justify">&nbsp;</P>

<P STYLE="font: 9pt Times New Roman, Times, Serif; margin: 0 4.5pt 0 0; text-align: justify">This press release contains forward-looking
